aria-hidden="true" class="simple-menu__body simple-menu__body--plain py-4th" style="display: none;"><li><a data-login-modal-toggle-allow-untrusted-user="true" data-event-click-target="concerns#new" class="c-midnight-100 action-bar__button text-lg ws-nw pl-half" ue=" login-modal-toggle" href="https://www.g2.com/survey_responses/8724153/concerns/new">Report a Concern</a></li><li data-product-admin-class-name="is-hidden-default" data-product-admin-id="79670" data-product-admin-model="Product" data-ue-widget="product-admin" class="x-product-admin-initialized"><a data-login-modal-toggle-allow-untrusted-user="true" data-event-click-target="official_responses#new" class="c-midnight-100 action-bar__button text-lg ws-nw pl-half" ue=" login-modal-toggle" href="https://www.g2.com/survey_responses/cj-affiliate-review-8724153/official_response/new"><span>Respond as CJ Affiliate</span></a></li></ul></div></div></div></div><div class="tags--teal"><div alt="Validated CJ Affiliate Reviewer" class="tag top x-tooltip-initialized" title="" ue="tooltip" data-tip-text="Validated through LinkedIn" aria-describedby="4xmdp7-tooltip" data-yeti-box="4xmdp7-tooltip" data-toggle="4xmdp7-tooltip" data-resize="4xmdp7-tooltip" data-tooltip="9fny41-tooltip"><div class="d-f ai-c">Validated Reviewer<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" contain="paint" buffered-rendering="static" viewBox="0 0 16 12" class="c-teal-100 tiny ml-half icon-checkmark-thick nessy-only" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" role="presentation"><path d="M13.333 0L6.667 6.667l-4-4L0 5.333 6.667 12 16 2.667z"></path></svg></div></div><div class="tag top x-tooltip-initialized" data-container="body" title="" ue="tooltip" data-tip-text="Organic review. This review was written entirely without invitation or incentive from G2, a seller, or an affiliate." aria-describedby="zrl1mf-tooltip" data-yeti-box="zrl1mf-tooltip" data-toggle="zrl1mf-tooltip" data-resize="zrl1mf-tooltip" data-tooltip="riqcvp-tooltip">Review source: Organic</div></div></div><div class="paper__bd"><div class="d-f mb-1"><div class="f-1 d-f ai-c mb-half-small-only"><div class="stars large xlarge--medium-down stars-0"></div><div class="time-stamp pl-4th ws-nw"><span><span class="x-current-review-date" data-poison-date=""><meta content="2023-10-13" itemprop="datePublished"><time datetime="2023-10-13">Oct 13, 2023</time></span></span></div></div></div><div class="d-f"><div class="f-1"><div data-poison=""><a class="pjax" href="https://www.g2.com/products/cj-affiliate/reviews/cj-affiliate-review-8724153"><div class="m-0 l2" itemprop="name">"Missing Funds and Unresponsive Customer Support"</div></a></div><div data-poison-text=""><div itemprop="reviewBody"><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you like best about CJ Affiliate?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">The ONLY thing I like about CJ.com is the common advantage of such affiliate platforms: it centralizes performance tracking and earnings from various campaigns into one account, reducing the need to interact with multiple companies or issue numerous invoices. However, the negatives have outweighed this sole benefit. After over a decade of affiliation, the severe issues I faced have led me to transition to direct affiliations with key companies. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about CJ Affiliate?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">I have been an affiliate with CJ.com for a decade now, and over the years I have always found their service to be lacking.
</p><p class="formatted-text">However, a recent incident has brought my concerns to a breaking point: at the end of August €7500, all being confirmed commissions set to be paid out, disappeared from my account with no trace or explanation.
</p><p class="formatted-text">Despite numerous emails and requests for explanations, I have yet to receive a satisfactory response.
</p><p class="formatted-text">
</p><p class="formatted-text">The support I have received has been lackluster at best. The affiliate support emails are disorganized and fail to address the core issue, leaving me in a loop of frustration. There seems to be a communication about some bank transfers, possibly three, initiated at the end of August, but none of them reached my bank account. My bank confirmed that no such transfers were received, and had there been any error in the details, the funds would have bounced back.
</p><p class="formatted-text">
</p><p class="formatted-text">I have repeatedly requested to speak to a payment department supervisor, to no avail. A few days ago, I was contacted by a team handling promotional campaigns for a publisher, and I seized the opportunity to report the issue once more and requested to be connected to a payment department supervisor. Yet again, my request was met with unhelpful responses that felt mocking rather than problem-solving.
</p><p class="formatted-text">
</p><p class="formatted-text">The lack of accountability and transparency from CJ.com has been appalling. Not only are my funds missing, but the inability to even discuss the issue with a responsible person is utterly disappointing. This incident has left me feeling helpless and exasperated. I share this experience as a cautionary tale to others who might consider joining CJ.com. The service, at least from my experience, has shown a lack of seriousness in addressing grave issues that affect the financial standings of their affiliates. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-8724153 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is CJ Affiliate solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">The only advantage is the centralization of affiliations into a single account. But since the earned money disappears without explanations, it's not worth it anyway. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex justify-between"><a class="link d-f ai-c x-show-more js-log-click x-toggle-class-initialized x-login-modal-toggle-initialized" ue="toggle-class login-modal-toggle"
